RESUMO 

O  objetivo  deste  trabalho  √©  oferecer  uma  base  de  conhecimentos  em  Educa√ß√£o 

Financeira,  para  docentes  do  ensino  m√©dio,  pois  um  dos  maiores  desafios  do 

desenvolvimento  da  Educa√ß√£o  Financeira  nas  escolas  passa  pela  necessidade  de 

capacita√ß√£o  dos  professores  das  redes de  ensino.  Neste  trabalho  ser√°  apresentado o 

desenvolvimento do conceito de Educa√ß√£o Financeira, as estrat√©gias nacionais para a 

inser√ß√£o de tal tema nas escolas brasileiras, desde a Lei de Diretrizes e Bases (LDB) at√© 

a  Base  Nacional  Comum  Curricular  (BNCC).  Ser√£o  realizados  esclarecimentos  em 

rela√ß√µes aos conceitos de Educa√ß√£o Financeira, a necessidade de uma educa√ß√£o cr√≠tica, 

com  foco  na  cidadania  e  o  uso  da  matem√°tica  financeira  como  ferramenta  de 

aprendizagem  para  a  Educa√ß√£o  Financeira.  A  apresenta√ß√£o  de  temas,  tais  como 

Planejamento Financeiro, juros simples e composto, rendas uniformes, Taxa b√°sica de 

Juros (SELIC), infla√ß√£o, Imposto de Renda, Cr√©dito e Investimentos, ser√° complementada 

pela abordagem de situa√ß√µes problemas reais, do cotidiano, atreladas a estes t√≥picos 

apresentando a matem√°tica relacionada com tema como meio de desenvolvimento da 

habilidade  financeira.  Nota-se  que  o  objetivo  desde  trabalho  √©  desenvolver  nos 

docentes  um  modo  de  pensar  financeiramente  mais  cr√≠tico,  contribuindo  para  sua

Palavras-chaves:  Forma√ß√£o  de  Professores,  Educa√ß√£o  Financeira,  Matem√°tica  Financeira,

ABSTRAT 

The objective of this work is to offer a knowledge base in Financial Education for high 

school  teachers,  as  one  of  the  biggest  challenges  in  the  development  of  Financial 

Education in schools is the need to train teachers from the different education systems. 

This  work  presents  development  of  the  concept  of  Financial  Education,  the  national 

strategies for the insertion of this topic in Brazilian schools, from the Law of Guidelines 

and Bases (from Portuguese: Leis de Diretrizes e Bases - LDB) to the Common National 

Curriculum  Base  (from  Portuguese:  base  Nacional  Comum  Curricular  -  BNCC). 

Clarifications will be made regarding the concepts of financial education, the need for 

critical education with a focus on citizenship and the use of financial mathematics as a 

learning  tool  for  Financial  Education.  The  presentation  of  topics  such  as  Financial 

Planning,  simple  and  compound  interest,  uniform  income,  Basic  Interest  Rate  (also 

known  as  SELIC  ‚Äì  a  Brazilian  federal  funds  rate),  inflation,  Income  Tax,  Credit  and 

Investments,  will  be  complemented  by  addressing  real,  everyday  problem  situations 

linked  to  these  topics,  presenting  subject-related  math  as  a  means  of  financial  skill 

development. It should be noted that the objective of this work is to develop in teachers 

a  more  financially  critical  way  of  thinking,  adding  to  their  awareness  of  financial 

education in order to contribute with the essential elements in the training of teachers, 

thus contributing to the development of financially literate students, Who are critical 

thinkers able to make healthy financial choices. 

Keywords: Teacher Training, Financial Education, Financial Mathematics, Financial Literacy, 

Financial Citizenship.

6.  Considera√ß√µes Finais
